### Traffic

<a id="traffic-control-help-2"></a>

[traffic_control.help](#traffic-control-help-2)
: * **Summary**: Help for specific commands (use help() or help(“method”) for more information)
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `methodName`: String

<a id="traffic-control-last-traffic-state-update-of-members"></a>

[traffic_control.last_traffic_state_update_of_members](#traffic-control-last-traffic-state-update-of-members)
: * **Summary**: Return the last traffic state update of the given members, per member
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `members`: [Seq[com.digitalasset.canton.topology.Member]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/topology/Member.html)
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.synchronizer.sequencer.traffic.SequencerTrafficStatus](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/traffic/SequencerTrafficStatus.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Use this command to get the last traffic state update of each member. It will be last updated when a member consumed traffic.
  ```

<a id="traffic-control-set-traffic-balance"></a>

[traffic_control.set_traffic_balance](#traffic-control-set-traffic-balance)
: * **Summary**: Set the traffic purchased entry of a member
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `member`: [com.digitalasset.canton.topology.Member](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/topology/Member.html)
      * `serial`: [com.digitalasset.canton.config.RequireTypes.PositiveInt](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/RequireTypes$$PositiveInt$.html)
      * `newBalance`: com.digitalasset.canton.config.RequireTypes.NonNegativeLong
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Use this command to set the new traffic purchased entry of a member.
   member: member for which the traffic purchased entry is to be set
   serial: serial number of the request, must be strictly greater than the latest update made for that member
   newBalance: new traffic purchased entry to be set
  <br/>
   returns: the max sequencing time used for the update
   After and only after that time, if the new balance still does not appear in the traffic state,
    the update can be considered failed and should be retried.
  ```

<a id="traffic-control-traffic-state-2"></a>

[traffic_control.traffic_state](#traffic-control-traffic-state-2)
: * **Summary**: Return the traffic state of the node
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `synchronizerId`: [com.digitalasset.canton.topology.SynchronizerId](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/topology/SynchronizerId.html)
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.protocol.TrafficState](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/sequencing/protocol/TrafficState.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Use this command to get the traffic state of the node at a given time for a specific synchronizer id.
  ```

<a id="traffic-control-traffic-state-of-all-members"></a>

[traffic_control.traffic_state_of_all_members](#traffic-control-traffic-state-of-all-members)
: * **Summary**: Return the traffic state of the all members.
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `latestApproximate`: Boolean
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.synchronizer.sequencer.traffic.SequencerTrafficStatus](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/traffic/SequencerTrafficStatus.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Use this command to get the traffic state of all members.
        Set latestApproximate to true to get an approximation of the traffic state (including base traffic)
        at the latest possible timestamp the sequencer can calculate it. This an approximation only because the sequencer
        may use its wall clock which could be beyond the synchronizer time.
  ```

<a id="traffic-control-traffic-state-of-members"></a>

[traffic_control.traffic_state_of_members](#traffic-control-traffic-state-of-members)
: * **Summary**: Return the traffic state of the given members
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `members`: [Seq[com.digitalasset.canton.topology.Member]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/topology/Member.html)
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.synchronizer.sequencer.traffic.SequencerTrafficStatus](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/traffic/SequencerTrafficStatus.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Use this command to get the traffic state of a list of members at the latest safe timestamp.
  ```

<a id="traffic-control-traffic-state-of-members-approximate"></a>

[traffic_control.traffic_state_of_members_approximate](#traffic-control-traffic-state-of-members-approximate)
: * **Summary**: Return the traffic state of the given members at the latest approximate time
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `members`: [Seq[com.digitalasset.canton.topology.Member]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/topology/Member.html)
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.synchronizer.sequencer.traffic.SequencerTrafficStatus](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/traffic/SequencerTrafficStatus.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Use this command to get the traffic state of a list of members using the latest possible time the sequencer can
        estimate the state.
        CAREFUL: The returned state is only an approximation in the future and might not be the actual correct state
        by the time this timestamp is reached by the synchronizer.
  ```

<a id="traffic-control-traffic-state-of-members-at-timestamp"></a>

[traffic_control.traffic_state_of_members_at_timestamp](#traffic-control-traffic-state-of-members-at-timestamp)
: * **Summary**: Return the traffic state of the given members at a specific timestamp
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `members`: [Seq[com.digitalasset.canton.topology.Member]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/topology/Member.html)
      * `timestamp`: [com.digitalasset.canton.data.CantonTimestamp](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/CantonTimestamp.html)
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.synchronizer.sequencer.traffic.SequencerTrafficStatus](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/synchronizer/sequencer/traffic/SequencerTrafficStatus.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Use this command to get the traffic state of specified members at a given timestamp.
  ```

### Database

<a id="db-help-1"></a>

[db.help](#db-help-1)
: * **Summary**: Help for specific commands (use help() or help(“method”) for more information)
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `methodName`: String

<a id="db-migrate-1"></a>

[db.migrate](#db-migrate-1)
: * **Summary**: Migrates the instance’s database if using a database storage
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  When instances reside on different nodes, their database migration can be run in parallel
  to save time. Please not that the migration commands must however must be run on each node
  individually, because remote migration through `participants.remote...` is not supported.
  ```

<a id="db-repair-migration-1"></a>

[db.repair_migration](#db-repair-migration-1)
: * **Summary**: Only use when advised - repairs the database migration of the instance’s database
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `force`: Boolean
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  In some rare cases, we change already applied database migration files in a new release and the repair
  command resets the checksums we use to ensure that in general already applied migration files have not been changed.
  You should only use `db.repair_migration` when advised and otherwise use it at your own risk - in the worst case running
  it may lead to data corruption when an incompatible database migration (one that should be rejected because
  the already applied database migration files have changed) is subsequently falsely applied.
  ```

### Health

<a id="health-active-1"></a>

[health.active](#health-active-1)
: * **Summary**: Check if the node is running and is the active instance (mediator, participant)
  * **Return type**:
    : * Boolean

<a id="health-dump-2"></a>

[health.dump](#health-dump-2)
: * **Summary**: Collect Canton system information to help diagnose issues
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `outputFile`: String
      * `timeout`: [com.digitalasset.canton.config.NonNegativeDuration](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/NonNegativeDuration.html)
      * `chunkSize`: Option[Int]
  * **Return type**:
    : * String
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Generates a comprehensive health report for the local Canton process and any connected remote nodes.
  <br/>
  The arguments are:
    - outputFile: Specifies the file path to save the report. If not set, a default path is used.
    - timeout: Sets a custom timeout for gathering data, useful for large reports from slow remote nodes.
    - chunkSize: Adjusts the data stream chunk size from remote nodes. Use this to prevent gRPC errors related to 'max inbound message size'
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-generate-encryption-key-1"></a>

[keys.secret.generate_encryption_key](#keys-secret-generate-encryption-key-1)
: * **Summary**: Generate new public/private key pair for encryption and store it in the vault
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `name`: String
      * `keySpec`: [Option[com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.EncryptionKeySpec]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/EncryptionKeySpec.html)
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.EncryptionPublicKey](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/EncryptionPublicKey.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  The optional name argument allows you to store an associated string for your convenience.
  The keySpec can be used to select a key specification, e.g., which elliptic curve to use, and the default spec is used if left unspecified.
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-generate-signing-key-1"></a>

[keys.secret.generate_signing_key](#keys-secret-generate-signing-key-1)
: * **Summary**: Generate new public/private key pair for signing and store it in the vault
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `name`: String
      * `usage`: [Set[com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.SigningKeyUsage]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/SigningKeyUsage.html)
      * `keySpec`: [Option[com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.SigningKeySpec]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/SigningKeySpec.html)
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.SigningPublicKey](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/SigningPublicKey.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  The optional name argument allows you to store an associated string for your convenience.
  The usage specifies the intended use for the signing key that can be:
   - Namespace: for the root namespace key that defines a node's identity and signs topology requests;
   - SequencerAuthentication: for a signing key that authenticates members of the network towards a sequencer;
   - Protocol: for a signing key that deals with all the signing that happens as part of the protocol.
  The keySpec can be used to select a key specification, e.g., which elliptic curve to use, and the default spec is used if left unspecified.
  ```

[keys.secret.get_wrapper_key_id](#keys-secret-get-wrapper-key-id-1)
: * **Summary**: Get the wrapper key id that is used for the encrypted private keys store
  * **Return type**:
    : * String

  * **Arguments**:

      * `name`: String

  ```none
  The optional name argument allows you to store an associated string for your convenience.
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-register-kms-signing-key-1"></a>

[keys.secret.register_kms_signing_key](#keys-secret-register-kms-signing-key-1)
: * **Summary**: Register the specified KMS signing key in canton storing its public information in the vault
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `kmsKeyId`: String
      * `usage`: [Set[com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.SigningKeyUsage]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/SigningKeyUsage.html)
      * `name`: String
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.SigningPublicKey](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/SigningPublicKey.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  The id for the KMS signing key.
  The usage specifies the intended use for the signing key that can be:
   - Namespace: for the root namespace key that defines a node's identity and signs topology requests;
   - SequencerAuthentication: for a signing key that authenticates members of the network towards a sequencer;
   - Protocol: for a signing key that deals with all the signing that happens as part of the protocol.
  The optional name argument allows you to store an associated string for your convenience.
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-rotate-kms-node-key-1"></a>

[keys.secret.rotate_kms_node_key](#keys-secret-rotate-kms-node-key-1)
: * **Summary**: Rotate a given node’s keypair with a new pre-generated KMS keypair
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `fingerprint`: String
      * `newKmsKeyId`: String
      * `name`: String
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.PublicKey](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/PublicKey.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Rotates an existing encryption or signing key stored externally in a KMS with a pre-generated
        key. NOTE: A namespace root signing key CANNOT be rotated by this command.
  The fingerprint of the key we want to rotate.
  The id of the new KMS key (e.g. Resource Name).
  An optional name for the new key.
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-rotate-node-key-1"></a>

[keys.secret.rotate_node_key](#keys-secret-rotate-node-key-1)
: * **Summary**: Rotate a node’s public/private key pair
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `fingerprint`: String
      * `name`: String
  * **Return type**:
    : * [com.digitalasset.canton.crypto.PublicKey](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/crypto/PublicKey.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Rotates an existing encryption or signing key. NOTE: A namespace root or intermediate
        signing key CANNOT be rotated by this command.
  The fingerprint of the key we want to rotate.
  An optional name for the new key.
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-rotate-node-keys-1"></a>

[keys.secret.rotate_node_keys](#keys-secret-rotate-node-keys-1)
: * **Summary**: Rotate the node’s public/private key pairs
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  For a participant node it rotates the signing and encryption key pair.
  For a sequencer or mediator node it rotates the signing key pair as those nodes do not have an encryption key pair.
  NOTE: Namespace root or intermediate signing keys are NOT rotated by this command.
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-rotate-wrapper-key-1"></a>

[keys.secret.rotate_wrapper_key](#keys-secret-rotate-wrapper-key-1)
: * **Summary**: Change the wrapper key for encrypted private keys store
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `newWrapperKeyId`: String
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Change the wrapper key (e.g. AWS KMS key) being used to encrypt the private keys in the store.
  newWrapperKeyId: The optional new wrapper key id to be used. If the wrapper key id is empty Canton will generate a new key based on the current configuration.
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-upload-1"></a>

[keys.secret.upload](#keys-secret-upload-1)
: * **Summary**: Upload a key pair
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `pairBytes`: com.google.protobuf.ByteString
      * `name`: Option[String]
      * `password`: Option[String]
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Upload the previously downloaded key pair.
  pairBytes: The binary representation of a previously downloaded key pair
  name: The (optional) descriptive name of the key pair
  password: Optional password to decrypt an encrypted key pair
  ```

<a id="keys-secret-upload-from-1"></a>

[keys.secret.upload_from](#keys-secret-upload-from-1)
: * **Summary**: Upload (load and import) a key pair from file
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `filename`: String
      * `name`: Option[String]
      * `password`: Option[String]
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Upload the previously downloaded key pair from a file.
  filename: The name of the file holding the key pair
  name: The (optional) descriptive name of the key pair
  password: Optional password to decrypt an encrypted key pair
  ```

### Sequencer Connection

<a id="sequencer-connection-get"></a>

[sequencer_connection.get](#sequencer-connection-get)
: * **Summary**: Get Sequencer Connection
  * **Return type**:
    : * [Option[com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.SequencerConnections]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/sequencing/SequencerConnections.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Use this command to get the currently configured sequencer connection details for this sequencer client. If this node has not yet been initialized, this will return None.
  ```

<a id="sequencer-connection-help"></a>

[sequencer_connection.help](#sequencer-connection-help)
: * **Summary**: Help for specific commands (use help() or help(“method”) for more information)
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `methodName`: String

<a id="sequencer-connection-logout"></a>

[sequencer_connection.logout](#sequencer-connection-logout)
: * **Summary**: Revoke this sequencer client node’s authentication tokens and close all the sequencers connections.
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  On all the sequencers, all existing authentication tokens for this sequencer client node will be revoked.
  Note that the node is not disconnected from the synchronizer; only the connections to the sequencers are closed.
  The node will automatically reopen connections, perform a challenge-response and obtain new tokens.
  ```

<a id="sequencer-connection-modify"></a>

[sequencer_connection.modify](#sequencer-connection-modify)
: * **Summary**: Modify Default Sequencer Connection
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `modifier`: [com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.SequencerConnection => com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.SequencerConnection](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/sequencing/SequencerConnection.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Modify sequencer connection details for this sequencer client node, by passing a modifier function that operates on the existing default connection.
  ```

<a id="sequencer-connection-modify-connections"></a>

[sequencer_connection.modify_connections](#sequencer-connection-modify-connections)
: * **Summary**: Modify Sequencer Connections
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `modifier`: [com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.SequencerConnections => com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.SequencerConnections](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/sequencing/SequencerConnections.html)
      * `validation`: [com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.SequencerConnectionValidation](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/sequencing/SequencerConnectionValidation.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Modify sequencer connection details for this sequencer client node, by passing a modifier function that operates on the existing connection configuration.
  ```

<a id="sequencer-connection-set"></a>

[sequencer_connection.set](#sequencer-connection-set)
: * **Summary**: Set Sequencer Connection
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `connections`: [com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.SequencerConnections](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/sequencing/SequencerConnections.html)
      * `validation`: [com.digitalasset.canton.sequencing.SequencerConnectionValidation](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/sequencing/SequencerConnectionValidation.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Set new sequencer connection details for this sequencer client node. This will replace any pre-configured connection details. This command will only work after the node has been initialized.
  ```

### Testing

<a id="pruning-clear-schedule-2"></a>

[pruning.clear_schedule](#pruning-clear-schedule-2)
: * **Summary**: Deactivate automatic pruning.

<a id="pruning-find-pruning-timestamp"></a>

[pruning.find_pruning_timestamp](#pruning-find-pruning-timestamp)
: * **Summary**: Obtain a timestamp at or near the beginning of mediator state
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `index`: [com.digitalasset.canton.config.RequireTypes.PositiveInt](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/RequireTypes$$PositiveInt$.html)
  * **Return type**:
    : * [Option[com.digitalasset.canton.data.CantonTimestamp]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/CantonTimestamp.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  This command provides insight into the current state of mediator pruning when called with
  the default value of `index` 1.
  When pruning the mediator manually via `prune_at` and with the intent to prune in batches, specify
  a value such as 1000 to obtain a pruning timestamp that corresponds to the "end" of the batch.
  ```

<a id="pruning-get-schedule-1"></a>

[pruning.get_schedule](#pruning-get-schedule-1)
: * **Summary**: Inspect the automatic pruning schedule.
  * **Return type**:
    : * [Option[com.digitalasset.canton.admin.api.client.data.PruningSchedule]](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/admin/api/client/data/PruningSchedule.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  The schedule consists of a "cron" expression and "max_duration" and "retention" durations. The cron string
  indicates the points in time at which pruning should begin in the GMT time zone, and the maximum duration
  indicates how long from the start time pruning is allowed to run as long as pruning has not finished pruning
  up to the specified retention period.
  Returns `None` if no schedule has been configured via `set_schedule` or if `clear_schedule` has been invoked.
  ```

<a id="pruning-help-2"></a>

[pruning.help](#pruning-help-2)
: * **Summary**: Help for specific commands (use help() or help(“method”) for more information)
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `methodName`: String

<a id="pruning-prune-1"></a>

[pruning.prune](#pruning-prune-1)
: * **Summary**: Prune the mediator of unnecessary data while keeping data for the default retention period
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  Removes unnecessary data from the Mediator that is earlier than the default retention period.
  The default retention period is set in the configuration of the canton node running this
  command under `parameters.retention-period-defaults.mediator`.
  ```

<a id="pruning-prune-at"></a>

[pruning.prune_at](#pruning-prune-at)
: * **Summary**: Prune the mediator of unnecessary data up to and including the given timestamp
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `timestamp`: [com.digitalasset.canton.data.CantonTimestamp](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/data/CantonTimestamp.html)

<a id="pruning-prune-with-retention-period"></a>

[pruning.prune_with_retention_period](#pruning-prune-with-retention-period)
: * **Summary**: Prune the mediator of unnecessary data while keeping data for the provided retention period
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `retentionPeriod`: scala.concurrent.duration.FiniteDuration

<a id="pruning-set-cron-1"></a>

[pruning.set_cron](#pruning-set-cron-1)
: * **Summary**: Modify the cron used by automatic pruning.
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `cron`: String
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  The schedule is specified in cron format and refers to pruning start times in the GMT time zone.
  This call returns an error if no schedule has been configured via `set_schedule` or if automatic
  pruning has been disabled via `clear_schedule`. Additionally if at the time of this modification, pruning is
  actively running, a best effort is made to pause pruning and restart according to the new schedule. This
  allows for the case that the new schedule no longer allows pruning at the current time.
  ```

<a id="pruning-set-max-duration-1"></a>

[pruning.set_max_duration](#pruning-set-max-duration-1)
: * **Summary**: Modify the maximum duration used by automatic pruning.
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `maxDuration`: [com.digitalasset.canton.config.PositiveDurationSeconds](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/PositiveDurationSeconds.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  The `maxDuration` is specified as a positive duration and has at most per-second granularity.
  This call returns an error if no schedule has been configured via `set_schedule` or if automatic
  pruning has been disabled via `clear_schedule`. Additionally if at the time of this modification, pruning is
  actively running, a best effort is made to pause pruning and restart according to the new schedule. This
  allows for the case that the new schedule no longer allows pruning at the current time.
  ```

<a id="pruning-set-retention-1"></a>

[pruning.set_retention](#pruning-set-retention-1)
: * **Summary**: Update the pruning retention used by automatic pruning.
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `retention`: [com.digitalasset.canton.config.PositiveDurationSeconds](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/PositiveDurationSeconds.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  The `retention` is specified as a positive duration and has at most per-second granularity.
  This call returns an error if no schedule has been configured via `set_schedule` or if automatic
  pruning has been disabled via `clear_schedule`. Additionally if at the time of this update, pruning is
  actively running, a best effort is made to pause pruning and restart with the newly specified retention.
  This allows for the case that the new retention mandates retaining more data than previously.
  ```

<a id="pruning-set-schedule-2"></a>

[pruning.set_schedule](#pruning-set-schedule-2)
: * **Summary**: Activate automatic pruning according to the specified schedule.
  * **Arguments**:
    : * `cron`: String
      * `maxDuration`: [com.digitalasset.canton.config.PositiveDurationSeconds](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/PositiveDurationSeconds.html)
      * `retention`: [com.digitalasset.canton.config.PositiveDurationSeconds](../scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/config/PositiveDurationSeconds.html)
  * **Description**:
  <br/>
  ```none
  The schedule is specified in cron format and "max_duration" and "retention" durations. The cron string indicates
  the points in time at which pruning should begin in the GMT time zone, and the maximum duration indicates how
  long from the start time pruning is allowed to run as long as pruning has not finished pruning up to the
  specified retention period.
  ```
